
HADOOP
######

###################################################

Para acessar o namenode via Browser
http://localhost:50070/dfshealth.html#tab-overview

###################################################

No caso de uma máquina/servidor com Hadoop instalado e configurado devemos iniciar os serviços.
###############################################################################################
start-dfs.sh   -> iniciará os serviços do namenode, datanode e secundary namenode se for o caso.
start-yarn.sh  -> iniciará o yarn para gestão dos jobs de map/reduce.
jps -> mostra os serviços que estão em execução. Por exemplo:

[feliciani@server ~]$ jps
7938 NodeManager
8292 Jps
7814 ResourceManager
7577 SecundaryNameNode
2541 AmbaryServer
7101 NameNode
7309 DataNode


No caso do hadoop no Docker Desktop
###################################

feliciani@LAPTOP-V176DRSL:/mnt/e/projetos/docker-spark/spark$docker exec -it namenode bash  ############ entra no container do namenode

root@namenode:/# hdfs dfs -ls /   ################################################## listando os diretórios
Found 3 items
drwxr-xr-x   - root supergroup          0 2021-07-21 14:59 /hbase
drwxrwxr-x   - root supergroup          0 2021-07-04 19:42 /tmp
drwxr-xr-x   - root supergroup          0 2021-07-15 14:17 /user

root@namenode:/# hdfs dfs -ls /user/ ################################################## listando os diretórios
Found 3 items
drwxr-xr-x   - root supergroup          0 2021-07-15 23:34 /user/feliciani
drwxr-xr-x   - root supergroup          0 2021-07-09 17:48 /user/hive
drwxr-xr-x   - root supergroup          0 2021-07-15 14:20 /user/root

root@namenode:/# hdfs dfs -mkdir /user/feliciani/bigdata  ################################################## criando o diretório bigdata

root@namenode:/# hdfs dfs -ls /user/feliciani/bigdata ################################################## listando o novo diretório

root@namenode:/# touch teste.txt  ################################################## criando um arquivo no local do container, fora do HDFS

root@namenode:/# ls -la teste.txt
-rw-r--r-- 1 root root 0 Jul 21 16:05 teste.txt ######################################( r= read, w=write, x= execute)

############################################################################################################################################################

O arquivo tem 10 posições que definem as permissões/privilégios em um arquivo ou diretório..
- indicação de que é um arquivo. (d significará diretorio, l de link simbólico)
rw- (owner) - 3 posições para o owner(dono do arquivo)(neste caso, ler e escrever)
r-- (grupo do usuário) - 3 posições do meio referem-se as permissões do grupo daquele usuário. (neste caso, apenas leitura)
r-- (as 3 últimas posições referem-se as permissões de qualquer outro usuário (neste caso, apenas leitura)

Neste exemplo apenas o owner pode ler e escrever.

############################################################################################################################################################

root@namenode:/# chmod 777 teste.txt ############################ dando permissão total a todos os usuários para ler, escrever e executar

root@namenode:/# ls -la teste.txt ############################ permissão total
-rwxrwxrwx 1 root root 0 Jul 21 16:05 teste.txt

root@namenode:/# chmod 740 teste.txt ############ O owner poderá ler, escrever e executar. O grupo pode apenas ler, outros usuários fora do grupo não terão permissões

root@namenode:/# ls -la teste.txt
-rwxr----- 1 root root 0 Jul 21 16:05 teste.txt  ############ modificação de permissão realizada com sucesso.


#################### No HDFS as permissões ocorrem da mesma forma. Abaixo são diretórios onde o Owner pode ler, escrever e executar, o usuário do grupo pode executar e ler, e outros usuários podem apenas executar.

root@namenode:/# hdfs dfs -ls /user
Found 3 items
drwxr-xr-x   - root supergroup          0 2021-07-21 16:03 /user/feliciani
drwxr-xr-x   - root supergroup          0 2021-07-09 17:48 /user/hive
drwxr-xr-x   - root supergroup          0 2021-07-15 14:20 /user/root

root@namenode:/# hdfs dfs -chmod 777 /user  ######################################### dando permissão total a todos os usuários

root@namenode:/# hdfs dfs -put /input/datasets/ml-100k/u.data /user/feliciani/bigdata ############################## copiando arquivo do local para o HDFS

root@namenode:/# hdfs dfs -ls /user/feliciani/bigdata
Found 1 items
-rw-r--r--   3 root supergroup    1979173 2021-07-21 16:49 /user/feliciani/bigdata/u.data ############################## o arquivo foi copiado

############################################################################################################################################################
Criado o grupo supergroup 
Setado para fazer 3 replicações do arquivo nos datanodes
Arquivo contém 1.9 MB
O Owner pode ler e escrever, o grupo (supergoup) e outros usuário podem apenas ler o arquivo
############################################################################################################################################################


root@namenode:/# hdfs dfs -du /user/feliciani/bigdata ########### Mostra o espaço que o diretório bigdata está ocupando no HDFS (1.9 MB)
1979173  /user/feliciani/bigdata/u.data

root@namenode:/# hdfs dfs -get /user/feliciani/bigdata/u.data /input/datasets ######### copiando o arquivo do HDFS para o Local /input/datasets do container ou server

## O Cliente consulta os metadados do NameNode para descobrir o endereço do arquivo no DataNode e solicitará que envie o arquivo para o local.

Relaciona o outro arquivo (u.data) que contém apenas um bloco.

O Status mostra agora 5 blocos no total.


#######################################################################################################################


############ Contém 2 arquivos

root@namenode:~# hdfs dfs -du /user/feliciani/bigdata
533444411  /user/feliciani/bigdata/ratings.csv
1979173    /user/feliciani/bigdata/u.data

root@namenode:~# hdfs dfs -count -q /user/feliciani/bigdata
        none             inf            none             inf            1            2          535423584 /user/feliciani/bigdata



root@namenode:~# hdfs getconf -confkey dfs.blocksize  ################## Tamanho do bloco que está configurado 128 MB por padrão
134217728

root@namenode:~# hdfs dfs -stat %o hdfs://localhost:8020/user/feliciani/bigdata/u.data ############## Tamanho do bloco que está configurado 128 MB por padrão
134217728

root@namenode:~# hdfs dfs -du -h /user/feliciani/bigdata

1.9 M    /user/feliciani/bigdata/u.data
